< review>
I bought a touring bike from Bike Attack to go directly on tour. Worst experience I have ever had with mechanics. I bought a surly disc trucker, pannier racks, helmet and a couple of other items.
My issues were:
1) They fitted racks which under load, stopped the front disc brake working. This could have been a fatality. They never apologized for their behavior, and although they refunded money from the racks, I still am angry about this incompetence.
2) They cross threaded the drive side pedal. Not really a problem as I put it on, but since then it was difficult to put the pedal on, finally resulting in the threads failing whilst on a ride resulting in a long walk, and a train ride followed by another walk. And the cost of a new crankset. Which leads me on to...
3) The drive side crank was overtightened so much that it broke my Park Tools crank puller!
The sales guy I dealt with was great, and the price was reasonable, but the mechanics were a disgrace, and the dealings that I had with them after discovering the problems were atrocious.< /review>

<text>I'm from the Bay Area and purchased a surface 604 shred to have shipped up here as I was unable to find any local shops that carried it. Though it didn't say so on the site at time of order, they were out of stock of the 14 amp/hr battery upgrade and offered a few recovery options including throwing in a second 10 amp/hr. battery which was a great deal and appreciated on my end.

{'time': 1600883066653, 'text': "Alyson, thank you for taking the time to share your opinion. This review was written a few years ago before we even started our construction, but we wanted to take the time to respond publicly to your concern about having more self storage in the City of Oakley. A fun fact: There are more self storage facilities in the United States than McDonalds, Burger King, and Wendy's combined. Why? Nearly 1 in 10 US households utilizes self storage. Given that Oakley is a quickly-growing city with an abundance of new homes, self storage is a valuable service for the community. It may seem like there are a lot of self storage facilities, but that is because there are also a lot of new families moving to the community (especially with major employers like Amazon coming to town).\n\nAt Cypress Self Storage, we are at the intersection of E. Cypress Rd. and Picasso. Many customers in our local neighborhood rely on our business for their storage needs, especially customers that live at Emerson Ranch, Delaney Park, Summerlake, and other nearby communities. Given the major railroad crossing at E. Cypress Rd. and Main St., it's a pain for customers to leave our local community because the road can get backed up, especially when they just want to quickly drop by to access their stored items. Moreover, we are just across the street from Iron House Elementary School. Busy parents can easily pull right into our facility after picking up or dropping off their children at school (of course, once school reopens). Customers benefit from storing their items close to home in their local community.\n\nAt Cypress Self Storage, we care about our local community and installed major improvements at our expense. We installed a brand new left turn lane, making it easy for members of the community to pull into our facility (or simply make a U-turn, if needed). At Cypress Self Storage, we installed substantial landscaping and spent substantial money making our facility architecturally beautiful. Our facility acts as a buffer between the railroad (and its associated noise) and the community, lowering noise. With nearly 1 in 10 US households renting a self storage unit, we are proud to be part of the community and offer our valuable service.\n\nWe realize that there are a variety of new self storage facilities in Oakley to choose from. That is great, in our opinion, because the consumer has choice and can choose the facility that is best from them. We wish all the other facilities all the best. < review>
Overall: super fresh, super tasty (can be expensive)

FOOD: omg, wow. So good . Every piece of nigiri was absolutely amazing. We had an assortment of fish and seriously, every single piece was delicious. My favorites were the toro, uni, salmon belly. But seriously all were great. I have to say that I was very impressed by how fresh everything was and the presentation of the food was still excellent.

LOCATION/SERVICE: a little hard to find lol. It's like in an alley and I only found it because of a sidewalk sign. The restaurant was clean and had great service. People there were very friendly and on top of it. We got our food quickly.

Would recommend if looking for delicious sushi and willing to pay< /review>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><user_name>Jessica C. Lee<//user_name>< review>
Checked out this place on a quiet Sunday during their soft open. Second branch of a popular SF spot. Wait staff was lovely and attentive and the co-owner was so welcoming and friendly, recommending a perfectly clean tasting sake and making us feel as if we'd sat down to dinner at a friend's house (who just happens to make amazing sushi). Sashimi was delicious and fresh, flown in from Japan daily! They will add omakase and other specials eventually. Rolls were on point, good balance of filling v. rice, great flavor, and easy to fit in my mouth. Get the tamago too, it was just oozing with umami. We got comped a tasty green tea cheesecake for dessert! All in all a satisfying meal and I'm looking forward to making this my regular sushi spot.< /review>

This was a really impressive restaurant. The menu had all the mainstays of Southern Californian Mexican food, but it was also packed with gems you don't often see at other places. The chiles g√ºeritos, stuffed with shrimp and cheese and roasted, were particularly impressive. I can imagine sitting at the bar and enjoying a large plate of these with a couple of cold beers. Our entrees were also wonderful: birria de chivo and tampique√±a, and the handmade tortillas really shone. The service was impeccable. Our server, a friendly young woman, readily and warmly provided recommendations, and she helped us find an out of the way outside table, in order to accommodate out large dog, whose birthday we were celebrating. We're looking forward to finding another excuse to come to Indio, so we can explore more of the extensive menu at this top-notch desert restaurant.<//Review>
